<h1 className={"openapi__heading"}>AddSandboxScanResult</h1>

<MethodEndpoint method={"post"} path={"/api/v32.07/sandbox"}></MethodEndpoint>



```
x-prisma-cloud-target-env: {"permission":"sandbox"}
```



Adds a sandbox scan result, the scan is augmented with geolocation data and returned to the client

## Request
